Title: 鼻

----

Title-ruby: <ruby><rb>鼻</rb><rt>はな</rt></ruby>

----

Title-english: The Nose

----

Author: 

<ruby><rb>芥川</rb><rt>あくたがわ</rt></ruby><ruby><rb>龍之介</rb><rt>りゅうのすけ</rt></ruby>

----

Author-english: Akutagawa Ryūnosuke

----

Blurb: A priest famous all over for his long nose, so long that it hangs below his chin, gets fed up and attempts primitive surgery.

----

Level: Intermediate

----

Premium: false

----
